<s> in the low panelled hall sittingroom of the burlacombe's farmhouse on the village green michael strangway a clerical collar round his throat and a dark norfolk jacket on his back is playing the flute before a very large framed photograph of a woman which is the only picture on the walls <\s>
<s> his age is about thirty five his figure thin and very upright and his clean shorn face thin upright narrow with long and rather pointed ears his dark hair is brushed in a coxcomb off his forehead <\s>
<s> a faint smile hovers about his lips that nature has made rather full and he has made thin as though keeping a hard secret but his bright grey eyes dark round the rim look out and upwards almost as if he were being crucified <\s>
<s> there is something about the whole of him that makes him seen not quite present <\s>
<s> a gentle creature burnt within <\s>
<s> a low broad window above a window seat forms the background to his figure and through its lattice panes are seen the outer gate and yew trees of a churchyard and the porch of a church bathed in may sunlight <\s>
<s> the front door at right angles to the window seat leads to the village green and a door on the left into the house <\s>
<s> it is the third movement of veracini's violin sonata that strangway plays <\s>

<s> in the low panelled hall sittingroom of the burlacombe's farmhouse on the village green michael strangway a clerical collar round his throat and a dark norfolk jacket on his back is playing the flute before a very large framed photograph of a woman which is the only picture on the walls <\s>
<s> his age is about thirty five his figure thin and very upright and his clean shorn face thin upright narrow with long and rather pointed ears his dark hair is brushed in a coxcomb off his forehead <\s>
<s> a faint smile hovers about his lips that nature has made rather full and he has made thin as though keeping a hard secret but his bright grey eyes dark round the rim look out and upwards almost as if he were being crucified <\s>
<s> there is something about the whole of him that makes him seen not quite present <\s>

<s> in the low panelled hall sittingroom of the burlacombe's farmhouse on the village green michael strangway a clerical collar round his throat and a dark norfolk jacket on his back is playing the flute before a very large framed photograph of a woman which is the only picture on the walls <\s>
<s> his age is about thirty five his figure thin and very upright and his clean shorn face thin upright narrow with long and rather pointed ears his dark hair is brushed in a coxcomb off his forehead <\s>
<s> a faint smile hovers about his lips that nature has made rather full and he has made thin as though keeping a hard secret but his bright grey eyes dark round the rim look out and upwards almost as if he were being crucified <\s>
<s> there is something about the whole of him that makes him seen not quite present <\s>

<s> the front door at right angles to the window seat leads to the village green and a door on the left into the house <\s>

<s> his age is about thirty five his figure thin and very upright and his clean shorn face thin upright narrow with long and rather pointed ears his dark hair is brushed in a coxcomb off his forehead <\s>
<s> a faint smile hovers about his lips that nature has made rather full and he has made thin as though keeping a hard secret but his bright grey eyes dark round the rim look out and upwards almost as if he were being crucified <\s>
<s> there is something about the whole of him that makes him seen not quite present <\s>
<s> a gentle creature burnt within <\s>
<s> a low broad window above a window seat forms the background to his figure and through its lattice panes are seen the outer gate and yew trees of a churchyard and the porch of a church bathed in may sunlight <\s>
<s> the front door at right angles to the window seat leads to the village green and a door on the left into the house <\s>
<s> it is the third movement of veracini's violin sonata that strangway plays <\s>
<s> his back is turned to the door into the house and he does not hear when it is opened and ivy burlacombe the farmer's daughter a girl of fourteen small and quiet as a mouse comes in a prayer book in one hand and in the other a gloss of water with wild orchis and a bit of deep pink hawthorn <\s>
<s> she sits down on the window seat and having opened her book sniffs at the flowers <\s>
<s> coming to the end of the movement strangway stops and looking up at the face on the wall heaves a long sigh <\s>
<s> from the seat i picked these for yu mr <\s>
<s> turning with a start ah <\s>
<s> he puts his flute down on a chair against the far wall where are the others <\s>
<s> as he speaks gladys freman a dark gipsyish girl and connie trustaford a fair stolid blue eyed saxon both about sixteen come in through the front door behind which they have evidently been listening <\s>
<s> they too have prayer books in their hands <\s>
<s> they sidle past ivy and also sit down under the window <\s>
<s> good morning gladys good morning connie <\s>
<s> he turns to a book case on a table against the far wall and taking out a book finds his place in it <\s>
<s> while he stands thus with his back to the girls mercy jarland comes in from the green <\s>
<s> she also is about sixteen with fair hair and china blue eyes <\s>
<s> she glides in quickly hiding something behind her and sits down on the seat next the door <\s>
<s> and at once there is a whispering <\s>
<s> turning to them good morning mercy <\s>
<s> now yesterday i was telling you what our lord's coming meant to the world <\s>
<s> i want you to understand that before he came there wasn't really love as we know it <\s>
<s> i don't mean to say that there weren't many good people but there wasn't love for the sake of loving <\s>
<s> d'you think you understand what i mean <\s>
<s> gladys's eyes are following a fly <\s>
<s> it isn't enough to love people because they're good to you or because in some way or other you're going to get something by it <\s>
<s> we have to love because we love loving <\s>
<s> that's the great thing without that we're nothing but pagans <\s>
<s> please what is pagans <\s>
<s> that's what the first christians called the people who lived in the villages and were not yet christians gladys <\s>
<s> we live in a village but we're christians <\s>

<s> the note of a cuckoo comes travelling <\s>

<s> well he was the best christian i think that ever lived simply full of love and joy <\s>

<s> put up with the truth for once <\s>
<s> his words rush out you are the thing that pelts the weak kicks women howls down free speech <\s>
<s> this to day and that to morrow <\s>
<s> spirit not the ghost of it <\s>
<s> if you're not meanness there's no such thing <\s>
<s> if you're not cowardice there is no cowardice above the growing fierceness of the hubbub patriotism there are two kinds that of our soldiers and this of mine <\s>

<s> to more swear to utter no more blasphemy against your country swear it <\s>
<s> my country is not yours <\s>
<s> mine is that great country which shall never take toll from the weakness of others <\s>

<s> you can break my head and my windows but don't think that you can break my faith <\s>
<s> you could never break or shake it if you were a million to one <\s>
<s> a girl with dark eyes and hair all wild leaps out from the crowd and shakes her fist at him <\s>
<s> you're friends with them that killed my lad <\s>
<s> more smiles down at her and she swiftly plucks the knife from the belt of a boy scout beside her smile you cur <\s>
<s> a violent rush and heave from behind flings more forward on to the steel <\s>
<s> he reels staggers back and falls down amongst the crowd <\s>
<s> a scream a sway a rush a hubbub of cries <\s>
<s> the chief student shouts above the riot steady <\s>
<s> the crowd falls back and two students bending over more lift his arms and head but they fall like lead <\s>
<s> desperately they test him for life <\s>
<s> by the lord it's over <\s>
<s> then begins a scared swaying out towards the window <\s>
<s> some one turns out the lights and in the darkness the crowd fast melts away <\s>
<s> the body of more lies in the gleam from a single chinese lantern <\s>
<s> muttering the words poor devil <\s>
<s> he kept his end up anyway <\s>
<s> the chief student picks from the floor a little abandoned union jack and lays it on more's breast <\s>
<s> then he too turns and rushes out <\s>
<s> and the body of more lies in the streak of light and flee noises in the street continue to rise <\s>
<s> the curtain falls but rises again almost at once <\s>
<s> aftermath a late spring dawn is just breaking <\s>
<s> against trees in leaf and blossom with the houses of a london square beyond suffused by the spreading glow is seen a dark life size statue on a granite pedestal <\s>
<s> in front is the broad dust dim pavement <\s>
<s> the light grows till the central words around the pedestal can be clearly read erected to the memory of stephen more faithful to his ideal high above the face of more looks straight before him with a faint smile <\s>
<s> on one shoulder and on his bare head two sparrows have perched and from the gardens behind comes the twittering and singing of birds <\s>

<s> in the low panelled hall sittingroom of the burlacombe's farmhouse on the village green michael strangway a clerical collar round his throat and a dark norfolk jacket on his back is playing the flute before a very large framed photograph of a woman which is the only picture on the walls <\s>
<s> his age is about thirty five his figure thin and very upright and his clean shorn face thin upright narrow with long and rather pointed ears his dark hair is brushed in a coxcomb off his forehead <\s>
<s> a faint smile hovers about his lips that nature has made rather full and he has made thin as though keeping a hard secret but his bright grey eyes dark round the rim look out and upwards almost as if he were being crucified <\s>

<s> in the low panelled hall sittingroom of the burlacombe's farmhouse on the village green michael strangway a clerical collar round his throat and a dark norfolk jacket on his back is playing the flute before a very large framed photograph of a woman which is the only picture on the walls <\s>
<s> his age is about thirty five his figure thin and very upright and his clean shorn face thin upright narrow with long and rather pointed ears his dark hair is brushed in a coxcomb off his forehead <\s>
<s> a faint smile hovers about his lips that nature has made rather full and he has made thin as though keeping a hard secret but his bright grey eyes dark round the rim look out and upwards almost as if he were being crucified <\s>
<s> there is something about the whole of him that makes him seen not quite present <\s>
<s> a gentle creature burnt within <\s>

<s> the front door at right angles to the window seat leads to the village green and a door on the left into the house <\s>
<s> it is the third movement of veracini's violin sonata that strangway plays <\s>

<s> in the low panelled hall sittingroom of the burlacombe's farmhouse on the village green michael strangway a clerical collar round his throat and a dark norfolk jacket on his back is playing the flute before a very large framed photograph of a woman which is the only picture on the walls <\s>
<s> his age is about thirty five his figure thin and very upright and his clean shorn face thin upright narrow with long and rather pointed ears his dark hair is brushed in a coxcomb off his forehead <\s>
<s> a faint smile hovers about his lips that nature has made rather full and he has made thin as though keeping a hard secret but his bright grey eyes dark round the rim look out and upwards almost as if he were being crucified <\s>
<s> there is something about the whole of him that makes him seen not quite present <\s>
<s> a gentle creature burnt within <\s>

<s> the front door at right angles to the window seat leads to the village green and a door on the left into the house <\s>
<s> it is the third movement of veracini's violin sonata that strangway plays <\s>

<s> in the low panelled hall sittingroom of the burlacombe's farmhouse on the village green michael strangway a clerical collar round his throat and a dark norfolk jacket on his back is playing the flute before a very large framed photograph of a woman which is the only picture on the walls <\s>
<s> his age is about thirty five his figure thin and very upright and his clean shorn face thin upright narrow with long and rather pointed ears his dark hair is brushed in a coxcomb off his forehead <\s>
<s> a faint smile hovers about his lips that nature has made rather full and he has made thin as though keeping a hard secret but his bright grey eyes dark round the rim look out and upwards almost as if he were being crucified <\s>
<s> there is something about the whole of him that makes him seen not quite present <\s>

<s> the front door at right angles to the window seat leads to the village green and a door on the left into the house <\s>

<s> in the low panelled hall sittingroom of the burlacombe's farmhouse on the village green michael strangway a clerical collar round his throat and a dark norfolk jacket on his back is playing the flute before a very large framed photograph of a woman which is the only picture on the walls <\s>
<s> his age is about thirty five his figure thin and very upright and his clean shorn face thin upright narrow with long and rather pointed ears his dark hair is brushed in a coxcomb off his forehead <\s>
<s> a faint smile hovers about his lips that nature has made rather full and he has made thin as though keeping a hard secret but his bright grey eyes dark round the rim look out and upwards almost as if he were being crucified <\s>

<s> his age is about thirty five his figure thin and very upright and his clean shorn face thin upright narrow with long and rather pointed ears his dark hair is brushed in a coxcomb off his forehead <\s>
<s> a faint smile hovers about his lips that nature has made rather full and he has made thin as though keeping a hard secret but his bright grey eyes dark round the rim look out and upwards almost as if he were being crucified <\s>
<s> there is something about the whole of him that makes him seen not quite present <\s>
<s> a gentle creature burnt within <\s>
<s> a low broad window above a window seat forms the background to his figure and through its lattice panes are seen the outer gate and yew trees of a churchyard and the porch of a church bathed in may sunlight <\s>
<s> the front door at right angles to the window seat leads to the village green and a door on the left into the house <\s>
<s> it is the third movement of veracini's violin sonata that strangway plays <\s>
<s> his back is turned to the door into the house and he does not hear when it is opened and ivy burlacombe the farmer's daughter a girl of fourteen small and quiet as a mouse comes in a prayer book in one hand and in the other a gloss of water with wild orchis and a bit of deep pink hawthorn <\s>
<s> she sits down on the window seat and having opened her book sniffs at the flowers <\s>
<s> coming to the end of the movement strangway stops and looking up at the face on the wall heaves a long sigh <\s>
<s> from the seat i picked these for yu mr <\s>
<s> turning with a start ah <\s>
<s> he puts his flute down on a chair against the far wall where are the others <\s>
<s> as he speaks gladys freman a dark gipsyish girl and connie trustaford a fair stolid blue eyed saxon both about sixteen come in through the front door behind which they have evidently been listening <\s>
<s> they too have prayer books in their hands <\s>
<s> they sidle past ivy and also sit down under the window <\s>
<s> good morning gladys good morning connie <\s>
<s> he turns to a book case on a table against the far wall and taking out a book finds his place in it <\s>
<s> while he stands thus with his back to the girls mercy jarland comes in from the green <\s>
<s> she also is about sixteen with fair hair and china blue eyes <\s>
<s> she glides in quickly hiding something behind her and sits down on the seat next the door <\s>
<s> and at once there is a whispering <\s>
<s> turning to them good morning mercy <\s>
<s> now yesterday i was telling you what our lord's coming meant to the world <\s>
<s> i want you to understand that before he came there wasn't really love as we know it <\s>
<s> i don't mean to say that there weren't many good people but there wasn't love for the sake of loving <\s>
<s> d'you think you understand what i mean <\s>
<s> gladys's eyes are following a fly <\s>
<s> it isn't enough to love people because they're good to you or because in some way or other you're going to get something by it <\s>
<s> we have to love because we love loving <\s>
<s> that's the great thing without that we're nothing but pagans <\s>
<s> please what is pagans <\s>
<s> that's what the first christians called the people who lived in the villages and were not yet christians gladys <\s>
<s> we live in a village but we're christians <\s>

<s> the note of a cuckoo comes travelling <\s>

<s> well he was the best christian i think that ever lived simply full of love and joy <\s>

<s> put up with the truth for once <\s>
<s> his words rush out you are the thing that pelts the weak kicks women howls down free speech <\s>
<s> this to day and that to morrow <\s>
<s> spirit not the ghost of it <\s>
<s> if you're not meanness there's no such thing <\s>
<s> if you're not cowardice there is no cowardice above the growing fierceness of the hubbub patriotism there are two kinds that of our soldiers and this of mine <\s>

<s> to more swear to utter no more blasphemy against your country swear it <\s>
<s> my country is not yours <\s>
<s> mine is that great country which shall never take toll from the weakness of others <\s>

<s> you can break my head and my windows but don't think that you can break my faith <\s>
<s> you could never break or shake it if you were a million to one <\s>
<s> a girl with dark eyes and hair all wild leaps out from the crowd and shakes her fist at him <\s>
<s> you're friends with them that killed my lad <\s>
<s> more smiles down at her and she swiftly plucks the knife from the belt of a boy scout beside her smile you cur <\s>
<s> a violent rush and heave from behind flings more forward on to the steel <\s>
<s> he reels staggers back and falls down amongst the crowd <\s>
<s> a scream a sway a rush a hubbub of cries <\s>
<s> the chief student shouts above the riot steady <\s>
<s> the crowd falls back and two students bending over more lift his arms and head but they fall like lead <\s>
<s> desperately they test him for life <\s>
<s> by the lord it's over <\s>
<s> then begins a scared swaying out towards the window <\s>
<s> some one turns out the lights and in the darkness the crowd fast melts away <\s>
<s> the body of more lies in the gleam from a single chinese lantern <\s>
<s> muttering the words poor devil <\s>
<s> he kept his end up anyway <\s>
<s> the chief student picks from the floor a little abandoned union jack and lays it on more's breast <\s>
<s> then he too turns and rushes out <\s>
<s> and the body of more lies in the streak of light and flee noises in the street continue to rise <\s>
<s> the curtain falls but rises again almost at once <\s>
<s> aftermath a late spring dawn is just breaking <\s>
<s> against trees in leaf and blossom with the houses of a london square beyond suffused by the spreading glow is seen a dark life size statue on a granite pedestal <\s>
<s> in front is the broad dust dim pavement <\s>
<s> the light grows till the central words around the pedestal can be clearly read erected to the memory of stephen more faithful to his ideal high above the face of more looks straight before him with a faint smile <\s>
<s> on one shoulder and on his bare head two sparrows have perched and from the gardens behind comes the twittering and singing of birds <\s>

<s> in the low panelled hall sittingroom of the burlacombe's farmhouse on the village green michael strangway a clerical collar round his throat and a dark norfolk jacket on his back is playing the flute before a very large framed photograph of a woman which is the only picture on the walls <\s>
<s> his age is about thirty five his figure thin and very upright and his clean shorn face thin upright narrow with long and rather pointed ears his dark hair is brushed in a coxcomb off his forehead <\s>
<s> a faint smile hovers about his lips that nature has made rather full and he has made thin as though keeping a hard secret but his bright grey eyes dark round the rim look out and upwards almost as if he were being crucified <\s>

<s> in the low panelled hall sittingroom of the burlacombe's farmhouse on the village green michael strangway a clerical collar round his throat and a dark norfolk jacket on his back is playing the flute before a very large framed photograph of a woman which is the only picture on the walls <\s>
<s> his age is about thirty five his figure thin and very upright and his clean shorn face thin upright narrow with long and rather pointed ears his dark hair is brushed in a coxcomb off his forehead <\s>
<s> a faint smile hovers about his lips that nature has made rather full and he has made thin as though keeping a hard secret but his bright grey eyes dark round the rim look out and upwards almost as if he were being crucified <\s>
<s> there is something about the whole of him that makes him seen not quite present <\s>
<s> a gentle creature burnt within <\s>

<s> the front door at right angles to the window seat leads to the village green and a door on the left into the house <\s>
<s> it is the third movement of veracini's violin sonata that strangway plays <\s>

<s> in the low panelled hall sittingroom of the burlacombe's farmhouse on the village green michael strangway a clerical collar round his throat and a dark norfolk jacket on his back is playing the flute before a very large framed photograph of a woman which is the only picture on the walls <\s>
<s> his age is about thirty five his figure thin and very upright and his clean shorn face thin upright narrow with long and rather pointed ears his dark hair is brushed in a coxcomb off his forehead <\s>
<s> a faint smile hovers about his lips that nature has made rather full and he has made thin as though keeping a hard secret but his bright grey eyes dark round the rim look out and upwards almost as if he were being crucified <\s>
<s> there is something about the whole of him that makes him seen not quite present <\s>
<s> a gentle creature burnt within <\s>

<s> the front door at right angles to the window seat leads to the village green and a door on the left into the house <\s>
<s> it is the third movement of veracini's violin sonata that strangway plays <\s>

<s> in the low panelled hall sittingroom of the burlacombe's farmhouse on the village green michael strangway a clerical collar round his throat and a dark norfolk jacket on his back is playing the flute before a very large framed photograph of a woman which is the only picture on the walls <\s>
<s> his age is about thirty five his figure thin and very upright and his clean shorn face thin upright narrow with long and rather pointed ears his dark hair is brushed in a coxcomb off his forehead <\s>
<s> a faint smile hovers about his lips that nature has made rather full and he has made thin as though keeping a hard secret but his bright grey eyes dark round the rim look out and upwards almost as if he were being crucified <\s>
<s> there is something about the whole of him that makes him seen not quite present <\s>

<s> the front door at right angles to the window seat leads to the village green and a door on the left into the house <\s>

<s> in the low panelled hall sittingroom of the burlacombe's farmhouse on the village green michael strangway a clerical collar round his throat and a dark norfolk jacket on his back is playing the flute before a very large framed photograph of a woman which is the only picture on the walls <\s>
<s> his age is about thirty five his figure thin and very upright and his clean shorn face thin upright narrow with long and rather pointed ears his dark hair is brushed in a coxcomb off his forehead <\s>
<s> a faint smile hovers about his lips that nature has made rather full and he has made thin as though keeping a hard secret but his bright grey eyes dark round the rim look out and upwards almost as if he were being crucified <\s>

<s> his age is about thirty five his figure thin and very upright and his clean shorn face thin upright narrow with long and rather pointed ears his dark hair is brushed in a coxcomb off his forehead <\s>
<s> a faint smile hovers about his lips that nature has made rather full and he has made thin as though keeping a hard secret but his bright grey eyes dark round the rim look out and upwards almost as if he were being crucified <\s>
<s> there is something about the whole of him that makes him seen not quite present <\s>
<s> a gentle creature burnt within <\s>
<s> a low broad window above a window seat forms the background to his figure and through its lattice panes are seen the outer gate and yew trees of a churchyard and the porch of a church bathed in may sunlight <\s>
<s> the front door at right angles to the window seat leads to the village green and a door on the left into the house <\s>
<s> it is the third movement of veracini's violin sonata that strangway plays <\s>
<s> his back is turned to the door into the house and he does not hear when it is opened and ivy burlacombe the farmer's daughter a girl of fourteen small and quiet as a mouse comes in a prayer book in one hand and in the other a gloss of water with wild orchis and a bit of deep pink hawthorn <\s>
<s> she sits down on the window seat and having opened her book sniffs at the flowers <\s>
<s> coming to the end of the movement strangway stops and looking up at the face on the wall heaves a long sigh <\s>
<s> from the seat i picked these for yu mr <\s>
<s> turning with a start ah <\s>
<s> he puts his flute down on a chair against the far wall where are the others <\s>
<s> as he speaks gladys freman a dark gipsyish girl and connie trustaford a fair stolid blue eyed saxon both about sixteen come in through the front door behind which they have evidently been listening <\s>
<s> they too have prayer books in their hands <\s>
<s> they sidle past ivy and also sit down under the window <\s>
<s> good morning gladys good morning connie <\s>
<s> he turns to a book case on a table against the far wall and taking out a book finds his place in it <\s>
<s> while he stands thus with his back to the girls mercy jarland comes in from the green <\s>
<s> she also is about sixteen with fair hair and china blue eyes <\s>
<s> she glides in quickly hiding something behind her and sits down on the seat next the door <\s>
<s> and at once there is a whispering <\s>
<s> turning to them good morning mercy <\s>
<s> now yesterday i was telling you what our lord's coming meant to the world <\s>
<s> i want you to understand that before he came there wasn't really love as we know it <\s>
<s> i don't mean to say that there weren't many good people but there wasn't love for the sake of loving <\s>
<s> d'you think you understand what i mean <\s>
<s> gladys's eyes are following a fly <\s>
<s> it isn't enough to love people because they're good to you or because in some way or other you're going to get something by it <\s>
<s> we have to love because we love loving <\s>
<s> that's the great thing without that we're nothing but pagans <\s>
<s> please what is pagans <\s>
<s> that's what the first christians called the people who lived in the villages and were not yet christians gladys <\s>
<s> we live in a village but we're christians <\s>

<s> the note of a cuckoo comes travelling <\s>

<s> well he was the best christian i think that ever lived simply full of love and joy <\s>

<s> put up with the truth for once <\s>
<s> his words rush out you are the thing that pelts the weak kicks women howls down free speech <\s>
<s> this to day and that to morrow <\s>
<s> spirit not the ghost of it <\s>
<s> if you're not meanness there's no such thing <\s>
<s> if you're not cowardice there is no cowardice above the growing fierceness of the hubbub patriotism there are two kinds that of our soldiers and this of mine <\s>

<s> to more swear to utter no more blasphemy against your country swear it <\s>
<s> my country is not yours <\s>
<s> mine is that great country which shall never take toll from the weakness of others <\s>

<s> you can break my head and my windows but don't think that you can break my faith <\s>
<s> you could never break or shake it if you were a million to one <\s>
<s> a girl with dark eyes and hair all wild leaps out from the crowd and shakes her fist at him <\s>
<s> you're friends with them that killed my lad <\s>
<s> more smiles down at her and she swiftly plucks the knife from the belt of a boy scout beside her smile you cur <\s>
<s> a violent rush and heave from behind flings more forward on to the steel <\s>
<s> he reels staggers back and falls down amongst the crowd <\s>
<s> a scream a sway a rush a hubbub of cries <\s>
<s> the chief student shouts above the riot steady <\s>
<s> the crowd falls back and two students bending over more lift his arms and head but they fall like lead <\s>
<s> desperately they test him for life <\s>
<s> by the lord it's over <\s>
<s> then begins a scared swaying out towards the window <\s>
<s> some one turns out the lights and in the darkness the crowd fast melts away <\s>
<s> the body of more lies in the gleam from a single chinese lantern <\s>
<s> muttering the words poor devil <\s>
<s> he kept his end up anyway <\s>
<s> the chief student picks from the floor a little abandoned union jack and lays it on more's breast <\s>
<s> then he too turns and rushes out <\s>
<s> and the body of more lies in the streak of light and flee noises in the street continue to rise <\s>
<s> the curtain falls but rises again almost at once <\s>
<s> aftermath a late spring dawn is just breaking <\s>
<s> against trees in leaf and blossom with the houses of a london square beyond suffused by the spreading glow is seen a dark life size statue on a granite pedestal <\s>
<s> in front is the broad dust dim pavement <\s>
<s> the light grows till the central words around the pedestal can be clearly read erected to the memory of stephen more faithful to his ideal high above the face of more looks straight before him with a faint smile <\s>
<s> on one shoulder and on his bare head two sparrows have perched and from the gardens behind comes the twittering and singing of birds <\s>

<s> in the low panelled hall sittingroom of the burlacombe's farmhouse on the village green michael strangway a clerical collar round his throat and a dark norfolk jacket on his back is playing the flute before a very large framed photograph of a woman which is the only picture on the walls <\s>
<s> his age is about thirty five his figure thin and very upright and his clean shorn face thin upright narrow with long and rather pointed ears his dark hair is brushed in a coxcomb off his forehead <\s>
<s> a faint smile hovers about his lips that nature has made rather full and he has made thin as though keeping a hard secret but his bright grey eyes dark round the rim look out and upwards almost as if he were being crucified <\s>

<s> in the low panelled hall sittingroom of the burlacombe's farmhouse on the village green michael strangway a clerical collar round his throat and a dark norfolk jacket on his back is playing the flute before a very large framed photograph of a woman which is the only picture on the walls <\s>
<s> his age is about thirty five his figure thin and very upright and his clean shorn face thin upright narrow with long and rather pointed ears his dark hair is brushed in a coxcomb off his forehead <\s>
<s> a faint smile hovers about his lips that nature has made rather full and he has made thin as though keeping a hard secret but his bright grey eyes dark round the rim look out and upwards almost as if he were being crucified <\s>
<s> there is something about the whole of him that makes him seen not quite present <\s>
<s> a gentle creature burnt within <\s>

<s> the front door at right angles to the window seat leads to the village green and a door on the left into the house <\s>
<s> it is the third movement of veracini's violin sonata that strangway plays <\s>

<s> in the low panelled hall sittingroom of the burlacombe's farmhouse on the village green michael strangway a clerical collar round his throat and a dark norfolk jacket on his back is playing the flute before a very large framed photograph of a woman which is the only picture on the walls <\s>
<s> his age is about thirty five his figure thin and very upright and his clean shorn face thin upright narrow with long and rather pointed ears his dark hair is brushed in a coxcomb off his forehead <\s>
<s> a faint smile hovers about his lips that nature has made rather full and he has made thin as though keeping a hard secret but his bright grey eyes dark round the rim look out and upwards almost as if he were being crucified <\s>
<s> there is something about the whole of him that makes him seen not quite present <\s>
<s> a gentle creature burnt within <\s>

<s> the front door at right angles to the window seat leads to the village green and a door on the left into the house <\s>
<s> it is the third movement of veracini's violin sonata that strangway plays <\s>

<s> in the low panelled hall sittingroom of the burlacombe's farmhouse on the village green michael strangway a clerical collar round his throat and a dark norfolk jacket on his back is playing the flute before a very large framed photograph of a woman which is the only picture on the walls <\s>
<s> his age is about thirty five his figure thin and very upright and his clean shorn face thin upright narrow with long and rather pointed ears his dark hair is brushed in a coxcomb off his forehead <\s>
<s> a faint smile hovers about his lips that nature has made rather full and he has made thin as though keeping a hard secret but his bright grey eyes dark round the rim look out and upwards almost as if he were being crucified <\s>
<s> there is something about the whole of him that makes him seen not quite present <\s>

<s> the front door at right angles to the window seat leads to the village green and a door on the left into the house <\s>

<s> in the low panelled hall sittingroom of the burlacombe's farmhouse on the village green michael strangway a clerical collar round his throat and a dark norfolk jacket on his back is playing the flute before a very large framed photograph of a woman which is the only picture on the walls <\s>
<s> his age is about thirty five his figure thin and very upright and his clean shorn face thin upright narrow with long and rather pointed ears his dark hair is brushed in a coxcomb off his forehead <\s>
<s> a faint smile hovers about his lips that nature has made rather full and he has made thin as though keeping a hard secret but his bright grey eyes dark round the rim look out and upwards almost as if he were being crucified <\s>

<s> his age is about thirty five his figure thin and very upright and his clean shorn face thin upright narrow with long and rather pointed ears his dark hair is brushed in a coxcomb off his forehead <\s>
<s> a faint smile hovers about his lips that nature has made rather full and he has made thin as though keeping a hard secret but his bright grey eyes dark round the rim look out and upwards almost as if he were being crucified <\s>
<s> there is something about the whole of him that makes him seen not quite present <\s>
<s> a gentle creature burnt within <\s>
<s> a low broad window above a window seat forms the background to his figure and through its lattice panes are seen the outer gate and yew trees of a churchyard and the porch of a church bathed in may sunlight <\s>
<s> the front door at right angles to the window seat leads to the village green and a door on the left into the house <\s>
<s> it is the third movement of veracini's violin sonata that strangway plays <\s>
<s> his back is turned to the door into the house and he does not hear when it is opened and ivy burlacombe the farmer's daughter a girl of fourteen small and quiet as a mouse comes in a prayer book in one hand and in the other a gloss of water with wild orchis and a bit of deep pink hawthorn <\s>
<s> she sits down on the window seat and having opened her book sniffs at the flowers <\s>
<s> coming to the end of the movement strangway stops and looking up at the face on the wall heaves a long sigh <\s>
<s> from the seat i picked these for yu mr <\s>
<s> turning with a start ah <\s>
<s> he puts his flute down on a chair against the far wall where are the others <\s>
<s> as he speaks gladys freman a dark gipsyish girl and connie trustaford a fair stolid blue eyed saxon both about sixteen come in through the front door behind which they have evidently been listening <\s>
<s> they too have prayer books in their hands <\s>
<s> they sidle past ivy and also sit down under the window <\s>
<s> good morning gladys good morning connie <\s>
<s> he turns to a book case on a table against the far wall and taking out a book finds his place in it <\s>
<s> while he stands thus with his back to the girls mercy jarland comes in from the green <\s>
<s> she also is about sixteen with fair hair and china blue eyes <\s>
<s> she glides in quickly hiding something behind her and sits down on the seat next the door <\s>
<s> and at once there is a whispering <\s>
<s> turning to them good morning mercy <\s>
<s> now yesterday i was telling you what our lord's coming meant to the world <\s>
<s> i want you to understand that before he came there wasn't really love as we know it <\s>
<s> i don't mean to say that there weren't many good people but there wasn't love for the sake of loving <\s>
<s> d'you think you understand what i mean <\s>
<s> gladys's eyes are following a fly <\s>
<s> it isn't enough to love people because they're good to you or because in some way or other you're going to get something by it <\s>
<s> we have to love because we love loving <\s>
<s> that's the great thing without that we're nothing but pagans <\s>
<s> please what is pagans <\s>
<s> that's what the first christians called the people who lived in the villages and were not yet christians gladys <\s>
<s> we live in a village but we're christians <\s>

<s> the note of a cuckoo comes travelling <\s>

<s> well he was the best christian i think that ever lived simply full of love and joy <\s>

<s> put up with the truth for once <\s>
<s> his words rush out you are the thing that pelts the weak kicks women howls down free speech <\s>
<s> this to day and that to morrow <\s>
<s> spirit not the ghost of it <\s>
<s> if you're not meanness there's no such thing <\s>
<s> if you're not cowardice there is no cowardice above the growing fierceness of the hubbub patriotism there are two kinds that of our soldiers and this of mine <\s>

<s> to more swear to utter no more blasphemy against your country swear it <\s>
<s> my country is not yours <\s>
<s> mine is that great country which shall never take toll from the weakness of others <\s>

<s> you can break my head and my windows but don't think that you can break my faith <\s>
<s> you could never break or shake it if you were a million to one <\s>
<s> a girl with dark eyes and hair all wild leaps out from the crowd and shakes her fist at him <\s>
<s> you're friends with them that killed my lad <\s>
<s> more smiles down at her and she swiftly plucks the knife from the belt of a boy scout beside her smile you cur <\s>
<s> a violent rush and heave from behind flings more forward on to the steel <\s>
<s> he reels staggers back and falls down amongst the crowd <\s>
<s> a scream a sway a rush a hubbub of cries <\s>
<s> the chief student shouts above the riot steady <\s>
<s> the crowd falls back and two students bending over more lift his arms and head but they fall like lead <\s>
<s> desperately they test him for life <\s>
<s> by the lord it's over <\s>
<s> then begins a scared swaying out towards the window <\s>
<s> some one turns out the lights and in the darkness the crowd fast melts away <\s>
<s> the body of more lies in the gleam from a single chinese lantern <\s>
<s> muttering the words poor devil <\s>
<s> he kept his end up anyway <\s>
<s> the chief student picks from the floor a little abandoned union jack and lays it on more's breast <\s>
<s> then he too turns and rushes out <\s>
<s> and the body of more lies in the streak of light and flee noises in the street continue to rise <\s>
<s> the curtain falls but rises again almost at once <\s>
<s> aftermath a late spring dawn is just breaking <\s>
<s> against trees in leaf and blossom with the houses of a london square beyond suffused by the spreading glow is seen a dark life size statue on a granite pedestal <\s>
<s> in front is the broad dust dim pavement <\s>
<s> the light grows till the central words around the pedestal can be clearly read erected to the memory of stephen more faithful to his ideal high above the face of more looks straight before him with a faint smile <\s>
<s> on one shoulder and on his bare head two sparrows have perched and from the gardens behind comes the twittering and singing of birds <\s>

<s> in the low panelled hall sittingroom of the burlacombe's farmhouse on the village green michael strangway a clerical collar round his throat and a dark norfolk jacket on his back is playing the flute before a very large framed photograph of a woman which is the only picture on the walls <\s>
<s> his age is about thirty five his figure thin and very upright and his clean shorn face thin upright narrow with long and rather pointed ears his dark hair is brushed in a coxcomb off his forehead <\s>
<s> a faint smile hovers about his lips that nature has made rather full and he has made thin as though keeping a hard secret but his bright grey eyes dark round the rim look out and upwards almost as if he were being crucified <\s>

<s> in the low panelled hall sittingroom of the burlacombe's farmhouse on the village green michael strangway a clerical collar round his throat and a dark norfolk jacket on his back is playing the flute before a very large framed photograph of a woman which is the only picture on the walls <\s>
<s> his age is about thirty five his figure thin and very upright and his clean shorn face thin upright narrow with long and rather pointed ears his dark hair is brushed in a coxcomb off his forehead <\s>
<s> a faint smile hovers about his lips that nature has made rather full and he has made thin as though keeping a hard secret but his bright grey eyes dark round the rim look out and upwards almost as if he were being crucified <\s>
<s> there is something about the whole of him that makes him seen not quite present <\s>
<s> a gentle creature burnt within <\s>

<s> the front door at right angles to the window seat leads to the village green and a door on the left into the house <\s>
<s> it is the third movement of veracini's violin sonata that strangway plays <\s>

<s> in the low panelled hall sittingroom of the burlacombe's farmhouse on the village green michael strangway a clerical collar round his throat and a dark norfolk jacket on his back is playing the flute before a very large framed photograph of a woman which is the only picture on the walls <\s>
<s> his age is about thirty five his figure thin and very upright and his clean shorn face thin upright narrow with long and rather pointed ears his dark hair is brushed in a coxcomb off his forehead <\s>
<s> a faint smile hovers about his lips that nature has made rather full and he has made thin as though keeping a hard secret but his bright grey eyes dark round the rim look out and upwards almost as if he were being crucified <\s>
<s> there is something about the whole of him that makes him seen not quite present <\s>
<s> a gentle creature burnt within <\s>

<s> the front door at right angles to the window seat leads to the village green and a door on the left into the house <\s>
<s> it is the third movement of veracini's violin sonata that strangway plays <\s>

<s> a bit o love act i it is ascension day in a village of the west <\s>
<s> in the low panelled hall sittingroom of the burlacombe's farmhouse on the village green michael strangway a clerical collar round his throat and a dark norfolk jacket on his back is playing the flute before a very large framed photograph of a woman which is the only picture on the walls <\s>
<s> his age is about thirty five his figure thin and very upright and his clean shorn face thin upright narrow with long and rather pointed ears his dark hair is brushed in a coxcomb off his forehead <\s>
<s> a faint smile hovers about his lips that nature has made rather full and he has made thin as though keeping a hard secret but his bright grey eyes dark round the rim look out and upwards almost as if he were being crucified <\s>
<s> there is something about the whole of him that makes him seen not quite present <\s>
<s> a gentle creature burnt within <\s>
<s> a low broad window above a window seat forms the background to his figure and through its lattice panes are seen the outer gate and yew trees of a churchyard and the porch of a church bathed in may sunlight <\s>
<s> the front door at right angles to the window seat leads to the village green and a door on the left into the house <\s>
<s> it is the third movement of veracini's violin sonata that strangway plays <\s>
